// \t"busy_anim"\t\t\t"Activity Name".\n
// \t"entry_anim"\t\t"Activity Name"\n
// \t"exit_anim"\t\t\t"Activity Name"\n
// \t"busy_sequence"\t\t"Sequence Name". If specified, this is used over the activity name. Specify it in the hint node.\n
// \t"entry_sequence"\t"Sequence Name". If specified, this is used over the entry anim.\n
// \t"exit_sequence"\t\t"Sequence Name". If specified, this is used over the exit anim.\n
// \t"min_time"\t\t\t"Minimum time to spend in this busy anim"\n
// \t"max_time"\t\t\t"Maximum time to spend in this busy anim"\t0 = only stop when interrupted by external event\n
// \t"interrupts"\t\tOne of:\n
// \t\t\t\t\t\t"BA_INT_NONE"\t\tbreak out only when time runs out. No external influence will break me out.\n
// \t\t\t\t\t\t"BA_INT_DANGER"\t\tbreak out of this anim only if threatened\n
// \t\t\t\t\t\t"BA_INT_PLAYER"\t\tbreak out of this anim if I can see the player, or I'm threatened\n
// \t\t\t\t\t\t"BA_INT_AMBUSH"\t\tsomeone please define this - I have no idea what it does\n
// \t\t\t\t\t\t"BA_INT_COMBAT"\t\tbreak out of this anim if combat occurs in my line of sight (bullet hits, grenades, etc), -OR- the max time is reached\n

Close the group automatically after a short wait (good for 'success' messages)
process
Close the group automatically when the associated parent process exits (good for sticky 'error' messages)
forever
Never close the group automatically (used to indicate an error like the process exiting unexpectedly)

IQCTabbedObject
IControlSelectionChangedListener
NotProcedural!!!
Default
Zero
Half
Playhead
Paste
Drop
Jitter
Smooth
Stagger
Hold
Release
Steady
Ramp
Round
Default: Blend each control towards that control's default/neutral value
Zero: Blend each control towards 0.0
Half: Blend each control towards 0.5
One: Blend each control towards 1.0
Playhead: Blend each control towards that control's current value
In: Blend each control towards that control's value at the start of the time selection
Out: Blend each control towards that control's value at the end of the time selection
Paste: Blend each control towards the values previously copied into the clipboard
Drop: Blend each control towards that control's values prior to starting the floating modification layer
Jitter: Blend each control towards a copy of the control's values that have had noise added to them
Smooth: Blend each control towards a smoothed copy of the control's values
Stagger: Retime each control by a random amount, to offset them from each other
Hold: Retime each control by shifting any animation in the falloff towards the hold region
Release: Retime each control by shifting any animation in the falloff away from the hold region
Steady: Retime each control's animation towards having a constant velocity
Ramp: Blend each control towards a linear falloff between the start and end of the time selection's hold region
Spline: Blend each control towards a spline fitted through the control's values at the bookmarked times
Round: Blend each control towards a spline fitted through the four time selection times

<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/REC-html40/strict.dtd">\n<html><head><meta name="qrichtext" content="1" /><style type="text/css">\np, li { white-space: pre-wrap; }\n</style></head><body style=" font-family:'MS Shell Dlg 2'; font-size:12pt; font-weight:72; font-style:normal;">\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Copy &amp; Paste timing and motion blocks from a KeyValues file into the text box below. Refer to the example data to the right for the general format of the data.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">The currently selected animation range is used to define the start and end frames which are adjusted and referred to by the cycle times defined below. The selected range can be modified by changing &quot;Frame Start&quot; and &quot;Frame End&quot; below.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Supported keys are listed below.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">PlaybackRate</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Playback rate is a single value which will cause the selected animation to run at the specified speed. Values less than 1 will cause the animation to run slower, values greater than one will cause the animation to run faster. e.g. A value of 2 will cause the animation to run twice as fast.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">SetPlaybackRate</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">SetPlaybackRate is a series of blocks that contain two values; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">Cycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> &amp; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">PlaybackRate</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">. The cycle values for each block must not be duplicated and must be specified in order. These blocks modify the playback rate for the specific portion of the animation controlled by cycle. Cycle values are in the range of [0, 1] where 0 is the first frame of the animation and 1 is the last frame of animation.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">OverrideMotion</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">OverrideMotion is a series of blocks that contain three supported values; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">StartCycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">, </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">EndCycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> &amp; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">MotionScale</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">. </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600; color:#aa0000;">Movement</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> parameters are ignored. OverrideMotion with a MotionScale value will scale the selectedtranslation values by the MotionScale value in the range of animation specified.</span></p></body></html>

ExportAnimDialog
TrimAnimWidget
No Trim
trimtype
Specify if the frame range of the animation data exported should be trimmed or not
Trim Type:
Trim To Shot With Handles
Export the animation for the duration of the shot only which is shown below
Trim To Shot
Export the animation as is
Shot Start Frame:
The frame rate of this SFM session
Frame Rate:
Export the animation for the duration of the shot but include user specified pre & post handles of user specified length
Handle Frames Pre:
The last frame of the shot
Shot End Frame:
The first frame of the shot
If "Trim Type" is "Trim To Shot With Handles", this value is added to "Shot End Frame" to determine the last frame of exported animation
Handle Frames Post:
handleframespre
If "Trim Type" is "Trim To Shot With Handles", this value is subtracted from "Shot Start Frame" to determine the first frame of exported animation
Export End Frame:
The starting frame to export, computed from the above choices
Export Start Frame:
handleframespost
Write out the exported animation in keyvalues2 format rather than binary
ascii
Ascii
The ending frame to export, computed from the above choices
